Page 463 

019996,003500:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM
019997,003501: 
019998,003502:                                                                                                  #  USER MUST SCHEDULE CALLS TO NVSUB SO THAT THERE IS NO CONFLICT OF USE OR
019999,003503:                                                                                                  #  CONFUSION TO OPERATOR. THE OLD GRABLOCK (INTERNAL/INTERNAL INTERLOCK)
020000,003504:                                                                                                  #  HAS BEEN REMOVED AND THE INTERNAL USER NO LONGER HAS THE PROTECTION THIS
020001,003505:                                                                                                  #  OFFERED.
020002,003506: 
020003,003507:                                                                                                  #  THERE ARE TWO WAYS A JOB CAN BE PUT TO SLEEP BY THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
020004,003508:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM.      1) BY ENDIDLE
020005,003509:                                                                                                  #                2) BY NVSUBUSY
020006,003510:                                                                                                  #  THE BASIC CONVENTION IS THAT ONLY ONE JOB WILL BE PERMITTED ASLEEP VIA
020007,003511:                                                                                                  #  THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM AT A TIME. IF A JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
020008,003512:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP BY MEANS OF (1) OR (2) AND THERE IS ALREADY A JOB ASLEEP THAT WAS
020009,003513:                                                                                                  #  PUT TO SLEEP BY (1) OR (2), THEN AN ABORT IS CAUSED.
020010,003514: 
020011,003515:                                                                                                  #  THE CALLING SEQUENCE FOR NVSUB IS
020012,003516:                                                                                                  #                        CAF             V/N
020013,003517:                                                                                                  #        L               TC              NVSUB
020014,003518:                                                                                                  #        L+1             RETURN HERE IF OPERATOR HAS INTERVENED
020015,003519:                                                                                                  #        L+2             RETURN HERE AFTER EXECUTION
020016,003520: 
020017,003521:                                                                                                  #  A ROUTINE CALLED NVSUBUSY IS PROVIDED (USE IS OPTIONAL) TO PUT
020018,003522:                                                                                                  #  YOUR JOB TO SLEEP UNTIL THE OPERATOR RELEASES THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
020019,003523:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM. NVSUBUSY ALSO TURNS ON THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT.
020020,003524:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
020021,003525:                                                                                                  #  SINCE JOBSLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
020022,003526: 
020023,003527:                                                                                                  #  THE CALLING SEQUENCE IS
020024,003528:                                                                                                  #        CAF     WAKEFCADR
020025,003529:                                                                                                  #        TC      NVSUBUSY
020026,003530: 
020027,003531: 
020028,003532:                                                                                                  #  .
020029,003533: 
020030,003534:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN AN INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS THE OPERATOR
020031,003535:                                                                                                  #  IS USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM (BY HIS OWN INITIATION). IT IS
020032,003536:                                                                                                  #  NOT INTENDED FOR USE WHEN ONE INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS ANOTHER INTERNAL 
020033,003537:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM.
020034,003538: 
020035,003539:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY ABORTS (WITH CODE 01206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
020036,003540:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP IN PINBALL. IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO NVSUBUSY
020037,003541:                                                                                                  #  WHEN
020038,003542:                                                                                                  #  1)    DSPLIST NOT= +0.  THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY OF THE DSPLIST
020039,003543:                                                                                                  #        IS EXCEEDED.
020040,003544:                                                                                                  #  2)    CADRSTOR NOT= +0.  THIS INDICATES THAT A JOB IS ALREADY USING

Page 464 

020042,003546:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE.  (+-NZ INDICATE A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDLE.)
020043,003547: 
020044,003548:    4437           44444        PRENVBSY           CS       2K+3                                  #  SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED
020045,003549:    4440           60002                           AD       Q                                     #  BANKS ONLY DESIRING THE FCADR OF (LOC
020046,003550:    4441           60004                           AD       FBANK                                 #  FROM WHICH THE TC PRENVBSY WAS DONE) -2
020047,003551:    4442           04635        NVSUBUSY           TC       POSTJUMP                              #  TO BE ENTERED.
020048,003552:    4443           10647                           CADR     NVSUBSY1                              
020049,003553:    4444           02003        2K+3               OCT      2003                                  
020050,003554: 
020051,003555:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBSY1 MUST BE IN BANK 27 OR LOWER, SO IT WILL PUT CALLER TO SLEEP
020052,003556:                                                                                                  #  WITH HIS PROPER SUPERBITS.
020053,003557: 
020054,003558: 04,2647                                           SETLOC   ENDSPMM    +1                         
020055,003559: 04,2647                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
020056,003560: 04,2647           54001        NVSUBSY1           TS       L                                     
020057,003561: 04,2650           04220                           TC       ISCADR+0                              #  ABORT IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0.
020058,003562: 04,2651           04224                           TC       ISLIST+0                              #  ABORT IF DSPLIST NOT= +0.
020059,003563: 04,2652           04374                           TC       RELDSPON                              
020060,003564: 04,2653           30001                           CA       L                                     
020061,003565: 04,2654           55043                           TS       DSPLIST                               
020062,003566: 04,2655           05133        ENDNVBSY           TC       JOBSLEEP                              
020063,003567: 
020064,003568:                                                                                                  #  NVSBWAIT IS A SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED BANKS ONLY. IF
020065,003569:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS NOT BUSY, IT EXECUTES V/N AND RETURNS TO L+1 (L= LOC FROM
020066,003570:                                                                                                  #  WHICH THE TC NVSBWAIT WAS DONE). IF SYSTEM IS BUSY, IT PUTS CALLING JOB
020067,003571:                                                                                                  #  TO SLEEP WITH L-1 GOING INTO LIST FOR EVENTUAL WAKING UP WHEN SYSTEM
020068,003572:                                                                                                  #  IS NOT BUSY.
020069,003573: 
020070,003574:    4445                                           SETLOC   NVSUBUSY   +3                         
020071,003575:    4445                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
020072,003576:    4445           22007        NVSBWAIT           LXCH     7                                     #  ZERO NVMONOPT OPTIONS
020073,003577:    4446           54123                           TS       NVTEMP                                
020074,003578:    4447           34736                           CAF      BIT14                                 
020075,003579:    4450           71021                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT
020076,003580:    4451           61012                           AD       DSPLOCK                               
020077,003581:    4452           10000                           CCS      A                                     
020078,003582:    4453           14455                           TCF      NVSBWT1                               #  BUSY
020079,003583:    4454           14164                           TCF      NVSBCOM                               #  FREE. NVSUB WILL SAVE L+1 FOR RETURN
020080,003584:                                                                                                  #  AFTER EXECUTION.
020081,003585:    4455           24002        NVSBWT1            INCR     Q                                     #  L+2. PRENVBSY WILL PUT L-1 INTO LIST AND
020082,003586:    4456           14437                           TCF      PRENVBSY                              #  GO TO SLEEP.
020083,003587: 
020084,003588:                                                                                                  #  RELDSP IS USED BY VBPROC, VBTERM, VBRQEXEC, VBRQWAIT, VBRELDSP, EXTENDED
020085,003589:                                                                                                  #  VERB DISPATCHER, VBRESEQ, RECALTST.
020086,003590:                                                                                                  #  RELDSP1 IS USED BY MONITOR SET UP, VBRELDSP.
020087,003591: 
020088,003592:    4457           56002        RELDSP             XCH      Q                                     #  SET DSPLOCK TO +0, TURN RELDSP LIGHT
020089,003593:    4460           54144                           TS       RELRET                                #  OFF, SEARCH DSPLIST
020090,003594:    4461           44736                           CS       BIT14

Page 465 

020092,003596:    4462           00004                           INHINT                                         
020093,003597:    4463           71021                           MASK     MONSAVE1

020232,003736:                                                                                                  #  ERROR LIGHT RESET (RSET) TURNS OFF,
020233,003737:                                                                                                  #  UPLINK ACTIVITY, AUTO, HOLD, FREE, OPERATOR ERROR,
020234,003738:                                                                                                  #  PROG ALM, TRACKER FAIL.
020235,003739:                                                                                                  #  LEAVES GIMBAL LOCK AND NO ATT ALONE.
020236,003740:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO ZEROES THE :TEST ALARM: OUT BIT, WHICH TURNS OFF STBY, RESTART.
020237,003741:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO SETS :CAUTION RESET: TO 1.
020238,003742:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO FORCES BIT 12 OF ALL DSPTAB ENTRIES TO 1.
020239,003743: 
020240,003744: 40,3603                                           SETLOC   DOPROC     +2
